<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1.01.</font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">&#160; Entry into a
Material Definitive Agreement</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Attached hereto as Exhibit 10.01 is a Standard Offer, Agreement and
Escrow Instructions for Purchase of Real Estate dated as of December 23, 2004
(the &#147;Agreement&#148;) by and between Guitar Center, Inc. (&#147;Guitar Center&#148;) and John
and Denise Gooden (collectively, the &#147;Seller&#148;) regarding a parcel of real
property located at 5775 Lindero Canyon Rd., Westlake
Village, CA 91362 (the &#147;Property&#148;).&#160; The
Property consists of three buildings (96,033 square feet in the aggregate and
87,509, 7,556 and 968 square feet individually).&#160; The Agreement calls for an all cash purchase
price of $12.2 million payable upon satisfaction of certain contingencies as
set forth in the Agreement.&#160; A $120,000
deposit became due upon execution of the Agreement, with the remaining $380,000
deposit to be funded within two business days following satisfactory completion
of the 60 day due diligence period.&#160; The
Property is being sold on an &#147;as is&#148; basis.&#160;
Following closing, the Seller intends to lease the main building from
Guitar Center at a lease rate of $53,000 per month, triple net for a period of
up to six months.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 9.01.</font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">  Financial Statements and Exhibits.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&nbsp;Exhibits</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Standard
Offer, Agreement and Escrow Instructions For Purchase
of Real Estate dated as of December 23, 2004 by and between Guitar Center, Inc.
and John and Denise Gooden regarding a parcel of real property located at 5775 Lindero Canyon Rd., Westlake Village, CA 91362.</font></p>

  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Title:</font></i></p>
  </td>
  <td width="40%" colspan="2" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:40.46%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Executive Vice President and<br>
  Chief Financial Officer</font></p>
  </td>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">STANDARD
OFFER, AGREEMENT AND ESCROW<br>
INSTRUCTIONS FOR PURCHASE OF REAL ESTATE</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(Non-Residential)</font></i></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIR Commercial Real
Estate Association</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Buyer.</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.1 &#160;</font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">Guitar Center, Inc. a Delaware Corporation&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;"> </font></font>, ( &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Buyer</font></b>&#148;)
hereby offers to purchase the real property, hereinafter described, from the
owner thereof (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Seller</font></b>&#148;)
(collectively, the &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Parties</font></b>&#148; or
individually, a &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Party</font></b>&#148;), through
an escrow (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Escrow</font></b>&#148;) to close <strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">30 or</font></strike>  <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">60&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u> days after the waiver or expiration of the
Buyer&#146;s Contingencies, <font color="red" style="color:red;">(unless a
different Closing date is established by mutual written agreement of the
Parties)</font>&#160; (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Expected
Closing Date</font></b>&#148;) to be held by <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">First American Title Company - Escrow&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;(&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Escrow Holder</font></b>&#148;) whose
address is <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">2829 Townsgate
Road., #103, Westlake Village, CA 91361&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;"> </font>, Phone No. <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;818-707-7019&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;, Facsimile No.  <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;818-449-4190&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>upon the terms and conditions set forth
in this agreement (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Agreement</font></b>&#148;).&#160; Buyer shall have the right to assign Buyer&#146;s
rights hereunder, but any such assignment shall not relieve Buyer of Buyer&#146;s
obligations herein unless Seller expressly releases Buyer.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.2 &#160;The term &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Date
of Agreement</font></b>&#148; as used herein shall be the date when by execution and
delivery (as defined in paragraph 20.2) of this document or a subsequent
counteroffer thereto, Buyer and Seller have reached agreement in writing
whereby Seller agrees to sell, and Buyer agrees to purchase, the Property upon
terms accepted by both Parties.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Property.</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.1 &#160;The real property (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Property</font></b>&#148;) that is the subject of this offer consists of
(insert a brief physical description) </font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">Three building structures of approximately 96,033 square
feet in aggregate situated on approximately 7.02 acres of land.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u></font> is located in the City of <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">Westlake Village&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>, County of <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">Los Angeles&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, State of <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">California&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;, is commonly known by the street address 
of <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">5775 Lindero Canyon Road, Westlake Village,
CA&nbsp;91362&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;
and is legally described as: <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">(to be inserted during Escrow)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>
(APN: <u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">2054-029-054&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;).</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.2 &#160;If the legal description of the Property is
not complete or is inaccurate, this Agreement shall not be invalid and the
legal description shall be completed or corrected to meet the requirements of </font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">First American Title Company - Mike Nuesca &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>
</font>(&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Title Company</font></b>&#148;), which shall issue the title policy
hereinafter described.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.3 &#160;The Property includes, at no additional cost
to Buyer, the permanent improvements thereon, including those items which
pursuant to applicable law are a part of the property, as well as the following
items, if any, owned by Seller and at present located on the Property: electrical
distribution systems (power panel, bus ducting, conduits, disconnects, lighting
fixtures); telephone distribution systems (lines, jacks and connections only);
space heaters; heating, ventilating, air conditioning equipment (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">HVAC</font></b>&#148;); air lines; fire sprinkler systems;
security and fire detection systems; carpets; window coverings; wall coverings;
and </font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">none.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" color="blue" face="Times New Roman" style="color:blue;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&
nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" color="blue" face="Times New Roman" style="color:blue;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&
nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" color="blue" face="Times New Roman" style="color:blue;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&n
bsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;(collectively, the &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Improvements</font></b>&#148;).</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.4 &#160;The fire sprinkler monitor:</font>&#61472;</font><font color="blue" face="Wingdings" style="color:blue;">o</font> is owned by Seller and included in the
Purchase Price, <font color="blue" face="Wingdings" style="color:blue;">o</font> is leased by Seller, and Buyer will need to
negotiate a new lease with the fire monitoring company, or <font color="blue" face="Wingdings" style="color:blue;">&#253;</font> ownership will be detemined during Escrow <font color="red" style="color:red;">but if ownership is determined to be that of
Seller, then ownership will be transferred to Buyer as part of the Purchase
Price at Closing</font>.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.5 &#160;Except as provided in Paragraph 2.3, the
Purchase Price does not include Seller&#146;s personal property, furniture and
furnishings, and </font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>
</font>all of which shall be removed by
Seller prior to Closing.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.75pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Purchase Price.</font></b></p>

Seller for the Property shall be $</font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">12,200,000.00&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;</font>, payable as follows:</p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.2 &#160;If Buyer is taking title to the Property
subject to, or assuming, an Existing Deed of Trust and such deed of trust
permits the beneficiary to demand payment of fees including, but not limited
to, points, processing fees, and appraisal fees as a condition to the transfer
of the Property, Buyer agrees to pay such fees up to a maximum of 1.5% of the
unpaid principal balance of the applicable Existing Note.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Deposits.</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">4.1&#160; </font></strike><strike><font color="red" face="Wingdings" style="color:red;">o</font><font color="red" style="color:red;">&#160; Buyer has delivered
to Broker a check in the sum of $<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;,
payable to Escrow Holder, to be held by Broker until both Parties have executed
this Agreement and the executed Agreement has been delivered to Escrow Holder, <u>or</u></font></strike> <font color="blue" face="Wingdings" style="color:blue;">&#253;</font>&nbsp;Buyer
shall deliver to Escrow Holder a check in the sum of $<u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">120,000.00&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>
<font color="red" style="color:red;">within five (5) business days following
the date</font> when both Parties
have executed this Agreement and the executed Agreement has been delivered to
Escrow Holder.&#160; When cashed, the check
shall be deposited into the Escrow&#146;s trust acount to be applied toward the
Purchase Price of the Property at the Closing.&#160;
Should Buyer and Seller not enter into an agreement for purchase and
sale, Buyer&#146;s check or funds shall, upon request by Buyer, be promptly returned
to Buyer.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.2 &#160;Additional deposits:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">(a) Within 5 business days after the Date of
Agreement, Buyer shall deposit with Escrow Holder the additional sum of $<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;to
be applied to the Purchase Price at the Closing.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">(b) Within 5 business days after the
contingencies discussed in paragraph 9.1 (a) through (k) are approved or
waived, Buyer shall deposit with Escrow Holder the additional sum of $<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;to
be applied to the Purchase Price at the Closing.</font></strike></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.3 &#160;Escrow Holder shall deposit the funds
deposited with it by Buyer pursuant to paragraphs 4.1 and 4.2 (collectively the
&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Deposit</font></b>&#148;), in a State or
Federally chartered bank in an interest bearing account whose term is
appropriate and consistent with the timing requirements of this transaction.
The interest therefrom shall accrue to the benefit of Buyer, who hereby
acknowledges that there may be penalties or interest forfeitures if the
applicable instrument is redeemed prior to its specified maturity.&#160; Buyer&#146;s Federal Tax Identification Number is&nbsp;</font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u></font>&nbsp;. NOTE: Such interest bearing account
cannot be opened until Buyer&#146;s Federal Tax Identification Number is provided.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">5.</font></strike></b><strike><font size="1" color="red" style="color:red;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font color="red" style="color:red;font-weight:bold;">Financing Contingency.&#160; </font></b><i><font color="red" style="color:red;font-style:italic;">(Strike if not applicable)</font></i></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5.1 &#160;This offer is contingent upon Buyer obtaining
from an insurance company, financial institution or other lender, a commitment
to lend to Buyer a sum equal to at least&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;%
of the Purchase Price, at terms reasonably acceptable to Buyer. Such loan (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">New Loan</font></b>&#148;) shall be secured by a first deed
of trust or mortgage on the Property. If this Agreement provides for Seller to
carry back junior financing, then Seller shall have the right to approve the
terms of the New Loan. Seller shall have 7 days from receipt of the commitment
setting forth the proposed terms of the New Loan to approve or disapprove of
such proposed terms. If Seller fails to notify Escrow Holder, in writing, of
the disapproval within said 7 days it shall be conclusively presumed that
Seller has approved the terms of the New Loan.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5.2 &#160;Buyer hereby agrees to diligently pursue
obtaining the New Loan.&#160;&#160; <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">If Buyer shall fail to notify its Broker, Escrow
Holder and Seller, in writing within&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
following the Date of Agreement, that the New Loan has not been obtained, it
shall be conclusively presumed that Buyer has either obtained said New Loan or
has waived this New Loan contingency.</font></b></font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;5.3 &#160;If, after due diligence, Buyer shall notify
its Broker, Escrow Holder and Seller, in writing, within the time specified in
paragraph 5.2 hereof, that Buyer has not obtained said New Loan, this Agreement
shall be terminated, and Buyer shall be entitled to the prompt return of the
Deposit, plus any interest earned thereon, less only Escrow Holder and Title
Company cancellation fees and costs, which Buyer shall pay.</font></strike></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">6.</font></strike></b><strike><font size="1" color="red" style="color:red;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font color="red" style="color:red;font-weight:bold;">Seller Financing&#160; </font></b><font color="red" style="color:red;">(Purchase Money Note).&#160;
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">(Strike if not applicable)</font></i></font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.1 &#160;The Purchase Money Note shall provide for
interest on unpaid principal at the rate of&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;%
per annum, with principal and interest paid as follows: <u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbs
p;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;.</u></font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><u><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&
nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;.</font></u></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><u><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&
nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;.</font></u></strike></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><u><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&n
bsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u><font color="red" style="color:red;">&nbsp;&nbsp;.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">The Purchase Money Note and Purchase Money Deed of Trust shall be on
the current forms commonly used by Escrow Holder, and be junior and subordinate
only to the Existing Note(s) and/or the New Loan expressly called for by this
Agreement.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.2 &#160;The Purchase Money Note and/or the Purchase
Money Deed of Trust shall contain provisions regarding the following (see also
paragraph 10.3 (b)):</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(a)
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Prepayment</font></i>. Principal may be
prepaid in whole or in part at any time without penalty, at the option of the
Buyer.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(b)
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Late Charge</font></i>. A late charge of 6%
shall be payable with respect to any payment of principal, interest, or other
charges, not made within 10 days after it is due.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;(c)
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Due On Sale</font></i>. In the event the
Buyer sells or transfers title to the Property or any portion thereof, then the
Seller may, at Seller&#146;s option, require the entire unpaid balance of said Note
to be paid in full.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;6.3 &#160;If the Purchase Money Deed of Trust is to be
subordinate to other financing, Escrow Holder shall, at Buyer&#146;s expense prepare
and record on Seller&#146;s behalf a request for notice of default and/or sale with
regard to each mortgage or deed of trust to which it will be subordinate.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.4 &#160;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">WARNING:
CALIFORNIA LAW DOES NOT ALLOW DEFICIENCY JUDGEMENTS ON SELLER FINANCING.&#160; IF BUYER ULTIMATELY DEFAULTS ON THE LOAN,
SELLER&#146;S SOLE REMEDY IS TO FORECLOSE ON THE PROPERTY.</font></b></font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.</font></b>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Real Estate Brokers.</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font>1&#160; The</font> following real estate broker(s) (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Brokers</font></b>&#148;)
and brokerage relationships exist in this transaction and are consented to by
the Parties (check the applicable boxes):</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.85pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.8pt;"><font size="2" color="blue" face="Wingdings" style="color:blue;font-size:10.0pt;">&#253;</font><font size="1" color="blue" style="color:blue;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">Level One Commercial Real Estate Services&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;
represents Seller exclusively (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Seller&#146;s Broker</font></b>&#148;);</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.85pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.8pt;"><font size="2" color="blue" face="Wingdings" style="color:blue;font-size:10.0pt;">&#253;</font><font size="1" color="blue" style="color:blue;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">CB Richard Ellis, Inc.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;
represents Buyer exclusively (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Buyer&#146;s Broker</font></b>&#148;); or</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.85pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.8pt;"><font size="2" color="blue" face="Wingdings" style="color:blue;font-size:10.0pt;">o</font><font size="1" color="blue" style="color:blue;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font color="blue" style="color:blue;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</font></u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;represents b
oth Seller and Buyer (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Dual Agency</font></b>&#148;).</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Parties acknowledge that Brokers are the procuring cause of this
Agreement. See paragraph 24 regarding the nature of a real estate agency
relationship. Buyer shall use the services of Buyer&#146;s Broker exclusively in
connection with any and all negotiations and offers with respect to the
Property for a period of 1 year from the date inserted for reference purposes
at the tope of page 1.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.2 &#160;Buyer and Seller each represent and warrant to
the other that he/she/it has had no dealings with any person, firm, broker or
finder in connection with the negotiation of this Agreement and/or the
consummation of the purchase and sale contemplated herein, other than the
Brokers named in paragraph 7.1, and no broker or other person, firm or entity,
other than said Brokers is/are entitled to any commission or finder&#146;s fee in
connection with this transaction as the result of any dealings or acts of such
Party. Buyer and Seller do each hereby agree to indemnify, defend, protect and
hold the other harmless from and against any costs, expenses or liability for
compensation, commission or charges which may be claimed by any broker, finder
or other similar party, other than said named Brokers by reason of any dealings
or act of the indemnifying Party.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">8.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Escrow and Closing.</font></b></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.1 &#160;Upon acceptance hereof by Seller, this
Agreement, including any counteroffers incorporated herein by the Parties,
shall constitute not only the agreement of purchase and sale between Buyer and
Seller, but also instructions to Escrow Holder for the consummation of the
Agreement through the Escrow. Escrow Holder shall not prepare any further
escrow instructions restating or amending the Agreement unless specifically so
instructed by the Parties </font><strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">or
a Broker herein</font></strike></font>.
Subject to the reasonable approval of the Parties, Escrow Holder may, however,
include its standard general escrow provisions.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.2&#160; As soon as practical after the receipt of
this Agreement and any relevant counteroffers, Escrow Holder shall ascertain the
Date of Agreement as defined in paragraphs 1.2 and 20.2 and advise the Parties
and Brokers, in writing, of the date ascertained.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.3 &#160;Escrow Holder is hereby authorized and
instructed to conduct the Escrow in accordance with this Agreement, applicable law
and custom and practice of the community in which Escrow Holder is located,
including any reporting requirements of the Internal Revenue Code. In the event
of a conflict between the law of the state where the Property is located and
the law of the state where the Escrow Holder is located, the law of the state
where the Property is located shall prevail.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.4 &#160;Subject to satisfaction of the contingencies
herein described, Escrow Holder shall close this escrow (the &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Closing</font></b>&#148;) by recording a general warranty
deed (a grant deed in California) and the other documents required to be
recorded, and by disbursing the funds and documents in accordance with this
Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.5 &#160;Buyer and Seller shall each pay one-half of
the Escrow Holder&#146;s charges and Seller shall pay the usual recording fees and
any required documentary transfer taxes. Seller shall pay the premium for a
standard coverage owner&#146;s or joint protection policy of title insurance.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.6 &#160;Escrow Holder shall verify that all of Buyer&#146;s
contingencies have been satisfied or waived prior to Closing. The matters
contained in paragraphs 9.1 subparagraphs (b), (c), (d), (e), (g), (i), (n),
and (o), 9.4, 9.5, 12, 13, 14, 16, 18, 20, 21, 22, and 24 are, however, matters
of agreement between the Parties only and are not instructions to Escrow
Holder.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.7 &#160;If this transaction is terminated for
non-satisfaction and non-waiver of a Buyer&#146;s Contingency, as defined in
paragraph 9.2, then neither of the Parties shall thereafter have any liability
to the other under this Agreement, except to the extent of a breach of any
affirmative covenant or warranty in this Agreement. In the event of such
termination, Buyer shall be promptly refunded all funds deposited by Buyer with
Escrow Holder, less only Title Company and Escrow Holder cancellation fees and
costs, all of which shall be Buyer&#146;s obligation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.8&#160; The Closing shall occur on the Expected
Closing Date, or as soon thereafter as the Escrow is in condition for Closing;
provided, however, that if the Closing does not occur by the Expected Closing
Date and said Date is not extended by mutual instructions of the Parties, a
Party not then in default under this Agreement may notify the other Party,
Escrow Holder, and Brokers, in writing that, unless the Closing occurs within 5
business days following said notice, the Escrow shall be deemed terminated
without further notice or instructions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.9&#160; Except as otherwise provided herein, the
termination of Escrow shall not relieve or release either Party from any
obligation to pay Escrow Holder&#146;s fees and costs or constitute a waiver,
release or discharge of any breach or default that has occurred in the
performance of the obligations, agreements, covenants or warranties contained
therein.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.10&#160; If this Escrow is terminated for any reason
other than Seller&#146;s breach or default, then at Seller&#146;s request, and as a
condition to the return of Buyer&#146;s deposit, Buyer shall within 5 days after
written request deliver to Seller, at no charge, copies of all surveys,
engineering studies, soil reports, maps, master plans, feasibility studies and
other similar items prepared by or for Buyer that pertain to the Property.
Provided, however, that Buyer shall not be required to deliver any such report
if the written contract which Buyer entered into with the consultant who
prepared such report specifically forbids the dissemination of the report to
others.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">9.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Contingencies to Closing.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.1 &#160;The Closing of this transaction is contingent
upon the satisfaction or waiver of the following contingencies. <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">IF BUYER FAILS TO NOTIFY ESCROW HOLDER, IN WRITING, OF
THE DISAPPROVAL OF ANY OF SAID CONTINGENCIES WITHIN THE TIME SPECIFIED THEREIN,
IT SHALL BE CONCLUSIVELY PRESUMED THAT BUYER HAS APPROVED SUCH ITEM, MATTER OR
DOCUMENT</font></b>. Buyer&#146;s conditional approval shall constitute disapproval,
unless provision is made by the Seller within the time specified therefore by
the Buyer in such conditional approval or by this Agreement, whichever is
later, for the satisfaction of the condition imposed by the Buyer. Escrow
Holder shall promptly provide all Parties with copies of any written
disapproval or conditional approval which it receives. With regard to
subparagraphs (a) through (l) the pre-printed time periods shall control unless
a different number of days is inserted in the spaces provided.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Disclosure</font></i>. Seller shall make to Buyer,
through escrow, all of the applicable disclosures required by law (See AIR
Commercial Real Estate Association (<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">&#147;AIR&#148;</font></b>)
standard form entitled &#147;Seller&#146;s Mandatory Disclosure Statement&#148;) and provide
Buyer with a completed Property Information Sheet (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Property Information Sheet</font></b>&#148;) concerning the Property, duly
executed by or on behalf of Seller in the current form or equivalent to that
published by the AIR </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">on or
before the opening of Escrow <strike>within 10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
following the Date of Agreement</strike></font></font>. Buyer has <font color="red" style="color:red;">60 <strike>10</strike></font> days from the receipt of said disclosures to
approve or disapprove the matters disclosed.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Physical Inspection</font></i>. Buyer has </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">the Due Diligence Period <strike>10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
from the receipt of the Property Information Sheet or the Date of Agreement,
whichever is later</strike></font><strike>,</strike></font> to satisfy itself with regard to the physical aspects and size of the
Property.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Hazardous Substance Conditions Repor</font></i>t.
Buyer has </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">the Due Diligence
Period <strike>30 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
from the receipt of the Property Information Sheet or the Date of Agreement,
whichever is later</strike></font>,</font> to satisfy itself with regard to the environmental aspects of the
Property. Seller <font color="red" style="color:red;">and the Brokers</font> recommend<strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">s</font></strike>
that Buyer obtain a Hazardous Substance Conditions Report concerning the
Property and relevant adjoining properties. Any such report shall be paid for
by Buyer. A &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Hazardous Substance</font></b>&#148;
for purposes of this Agreement is defined as any substance whose nature and/or
quantity of existence, use, manufacture, disposal or effect, render it subject
to Federal, state or local regulation, investigation, remediation or removal as
potentially injurious to public health or welfare. A &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Hazardous Substance Condition</font></b>&#148; for purposes
of this Agreement is defined as the existence on, under or relevantly adjacent
to the Property of a Hazardous Substance that would require remediation and/or
removal under applicable Federal, state or local law.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Soil Inspection</font></i>. Buyer&#160; has </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">the Due Diligence Period <strike>30 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
from the receipt of the Property Information Sheet or the Date of Agreement,
whichever is later</strike></font>,</font> to satisfy itself with regard to the condition of the soils on the
Property. Seller recommends that Buyer obtain a soil test report. Any such
report shall be paid for by Buyer. Seller shall provide Buyer copies of any
soils report that Seller may have within 10 days of the Date of Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Governmental Approvals</font></i>. Buyer has </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">the Due Diligence Period <strike>30 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
from the Date of Agreement</strike></font></font> to satisfy itself with regard to approvals and permits from
governmental agencies or departments which have or may have jurisdiction over
the Property and which Buyer deems necessary or desirable in connection with
its intended use of the Property, including, but not limited to, permits and
approvals required with respect to zoning, planning, building and safety, fire,
police, handicapped and Americans with Disabilities Act requirements,
transportation and environmental matters.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Conditions of Title</font></i>. Escrow Holder shall
cause a current commitment for title insurance (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Title Commitment</font></b>&#148;) concerning the Property issued by the Title
Company, as well as legible copies of all documents referred to in the Title
Commitment (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Underlying Documents</font></b>&#148;)
to be delivered to Buyer within </font>10 <font color="red" style="color:red;">days following the opening of Escrow <strike>or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
following the Date of Agreement</strike></font></font>. Buyer has <font color="red" style="color:red;">the Due
Diligence Period <strike>10 days from the receipt of the Title Commitment and
Underlying Documents</strike></font>
to satisfy itself with regard to the condition of title. The disapproval of
Buyer of any monetary encumbrance, which by the terms of this Agreement is not
to remain against the Property after the Closing, shall not be considered a
failure of this contingency, as Seller shall have the obligation, at Seller&#146;s
expense, to satisfy and remove such disapproved monetary encumbrance at or
before the Closing.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Survey</font></i>. Buyer has </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">the Due Diligence Period <strike>30 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
from the receipt of the Title Commitment and Underlying Documents</strike></font></font> to satisfy itself with regard to any ALTA
title supplement based upon a survey prepared to American Land Title
Association (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">ALTA</font></b>&#148;) standards for
an owner&#146;s policy by a licensed surveyor, showing the legal description and
boundary lines of the Property, any easements of record, and any improvements,
poles, structures and things located within 10 feet of either side of the
Property boundary lines. Any such survey shall be prepared at Buyer&#146;s direction
and expense. If Buyer has obtained a survey and approved the ALTA title
supplement, Buyer may elect within the period allowed for Buyer&#146;s approval of a
survey to have an ALTA extended coverage owner&#146;s form of title policy, in which
event Buyer shall pay any additional premium attributable thereto.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(h) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Existing Leases and Tenancy Statements</font></i>.
Seller shall </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">on or before the
opening of Escrow <strike>within 10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
of the Date of Agreement</strike></font></font> provide both Buyer and Escrow Holder with legible copies of all leases,
subleases or rental arrangements (collectively, &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Existing Leases</font></b>&#148;) affecting the Property, and with a tenancy
statement (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Estoppel Certificate</font></b>&#148;)
in the latest form or equivalent to that published by the AIR, executed by
Seller and/or each tenant and subtenant of the Property. Seller shall use its
best efforts to have each tenant complete and execute an Estoppel Certificate.
If any tenant fails or refuses to provide an Estoppel Certificate then Seller
shall complete and execute an Estoppel Certificate for that tenancy. Buyer has
10 days from the receipt of said Existing Leases and Estoppel Certificates to
satisfy itself with regard to the Existing Leases and any other tenancy issues.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Other Agreements</font></i>. Seller shall </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">on or before the opening of Escrow <strike>within
10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
of the Date of Agreement</strike></font></font> provide Buyer with legible copies of all other agreements (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Other Agreements</font></b>&#148;) known to Seller that
will affect the Property after Closing <font color="red" style="color:red;">including without limitation all service contracts and the
parking Sublease between Safe Publishing Company Inc. and BankCard USA Merchant
Services Inc. (the &#147;Parking Sublease&#148;)</font>. Buyer&#160; has <font color="red" style="color:red;">the Due Diligence Period <strike>10 days from the
receipt of said Other Agreements</strike></font>&#160; to satisfy itself with regard to
such Agreements.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(j) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Financing</font></i>. If paragraph 5 hereof dealing
with a financing contingency has not been stricken, the satisfaction or waiver
of such New Loan contingency.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">(<strike>k) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Existing
Notes</font></i>. If paragraph 3.1(c) has not been stricken, Seller shall
within 10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
of the Date of Agreement provide Buyer with legible copies of the Existing
Notes, Existing Deeds of Trust and related agreements (collectively, &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Loan Documents</font></b>&#148;) to which the Property will
remain subject after the Closing. Escrow Holder shall promptly request from the
holders of the Existing Notes a beneficiary statement (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Beneficiary Statement</font></b>&#148;) confirming: (1) the
amount of the unpaid principal balance, the current interest rate, and the date
to which interest is paid, and (2) the nature and amount of any impounds held
by the beneficiary in connection with such loan. Buyer has 10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
from the receipt of the Loan Documents and Beneficiary Statements to satisfy
itself with regard to such financing. Buyer&#146;s obligation to close is
conditioned upon Buyer being able to purchase the Property without acceleration
or change in the terms of any Existing Notes or charges to Buyer except as
otherwise provided in this Agreement or approved by Buyer, provided, however,
Buyer shall pay the transfer fee referred to in paragraph 3.2 hereof.</strike></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">(l) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Personal
Property</font></i>. In the event that any personal property is included in the
Purchase Price, Buyer has 10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
from the Date of Agreement to satisfy itself with regard to the title condition
of such personal property. Seller recommends that Buyer obtain a UCC-1 report.
Any such report shall be paid for by Buyer. Seller shall provide Buyer copies
of any liens or encumbrances affecting such personal property that it is aware
of within 10 or&nbsp;<u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u>&nbsp;days
of the Date of Agreement.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(m) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Destruction, Damage or Loss</font></i>.&#160; There shall not have occurred prior to the
Closing, a destruction of, or damage or loss to, the Property or</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">any portion thereof, from any cause whatsoever, which would cost more than&#160; </font><strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">$10,000.00</font></strike></font> <font color="red" style="color:red;">$50,000.00</font> to repair or cure. If the cost of repair or
cure is <strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">$10,000.00</font></strike><font color="red" style="color:red;"> $50,000.00</font> or less, Seller shall repair or cure the loss
prior to the Closing. Buyer shall have the option, within 10 days after receipt
of written notice of a loss costing more than&#160;
<strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">$10,000.00</font></strike><font color="red" style="color:red;"> $50,000.00</font> to repair or cure, to either terminate this
transaction or to purchase the Property notwithstanding such loss, but without
deduction or offset against the Purchase Price <font color="red" style="color:red;">except for the amount of Seller&#146;s insurance deductible</font>. If the cost to repair or cure is more
than&#160; <strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">$10,000.00</font></strike><font color="red" style="color:red;"> $50,000.00</font>, and Buyer does not elect to terminate this transaction, Buyer shall be
entitled to any insurance proceeds applicable to such loss. Unless otherwise
notified in writing, Escrow Holder shall assume no such destruction, damage or
loss has occurred prior to Closing.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(n) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Material Change</font></i>. Buyer shall have 10 days
following receipt of written notice of a Material Change within which to
satisfy itself with regard to such change. &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Material
Change</font></b>&#148; shall mean a change in the status of the use, occupancy,
tenants, or condition of the Property that occurs after the date of this offer
and prior to the Closing. Unless otherwise notified in writing, Escrow Holder
shall assume that no Material Change has occurred prior to the Closing.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(o) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Seller Performance</font></i>. The delivery of all
documents and the due performance by Seller of each and every undertaking and
agreement to be performed by Seller under this Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(p) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Warranties</font></i>. That each representation and
warranty of Seller herein</font><font color="red" style="color:red;">, if
any,</font></font> be true and
correct as of the Closing. Escrow Holder shall assume that this condition has
been satisfied unless notified to the contrary in writing by any Party prior to
the Closing.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(q) <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Brokerage Fee</font></i>. Payment at the Closing of
such brokerage fee as is specified in this Agreement or later written
instructions to Escrow Holder executed by Seller and Brokers (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Brokerage Fee</font></b>&#148;). It is agreed by the
Parties and Escrow Holder that Brokers are a third party beneficiary of this
Agreement insofar as the Brokerage Fee is concerned, and that no change shall
be made with respect to the payment of the Brokerage Fee specified in this
Agreement, without the written consent of Brokers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.2 &#160;All of the contingencies specified in subparagraphs
(a) through (p) of paragraph 9.1 are for the benefit of, and may be waived by,
Buyer, and may be elsewhere herein referred to as &#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Buyer&#146;s Contingencies</font></b>.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.3 &#160;If any Buyer&#146;s Contingency or any other matter
subject to Buyer&#146;s approval is disapproved as provided for herein in a timely
manner (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Disapproved Item</font></b>&#148;),
Seller shall have the right within 10 days following the receipt of notice of
Buyer&#146;s disapproval to elect to cure such Disapproved Item prior to the
Expected Closing Date (&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Seller&#146;s Election</font></b>&#148;).
Seller&#146;s failure to give to Buyer within such period, written notice of
Seller&#146;s commitment to cure such Disapproved Item on or before the Expected
Closing Date shall be conclusively presumed to be Seller&#146;s Election not to cure
such Disapproved Item. If Seller elects, either by written notice or failure to
give written notice, not to cure a Disapproved Item, Buyer shall have the
election, within 10 days after Seller&#146;s Election to either accept title to the
Property subject to such Disapproved Item, or to terminate this transaction.
Buyer&#146;s failure to notify Seller in writing of Buyer&#146;s election to accept title
to the Property subject to the Disapproved Item without deduction or offset
shall constitute Buyer&#146;s election to terminate this transaction. Unless
expressly provided otherwise herein, Seller&#146;s right to cure shall not apply to
the remediation of Hazardous Substance Conditions or to the Financing
Contingency. Unless the Parties mutually instruct otherwise, if the time
periods for the satisfaction of contingencies or for Seller&#146;s and Buyer&#146;s said
Elections would expire on a date after the Expected Closing Date, the Expected
Closing Date shall be deemed extended for 3 business days following the
expiration of: (a) the applicable contingency period(s), (b) the period within
which the Seller may elect to cure the Disapproved Item, or (c) if Seller
elects not to cure, the period within which Buyer may elect to proceed with
this transaction, whichever is later.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.4&#160; Buyer understands and agrees that </font><font color="red" style="color:red;">during the Due Diligence Period&#160; <strike>until such time as all Buyer&#146;s
Contingencies have been satisfied or waived</strike></font></font>, Seller and/or its agents may solicit, entertain <font color="red" style="color:red;">but not <strike>and/or</strike></font> accept back-up offers to purchase the Property.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.5&#160; The Parties acknowledge that extensive local,
state and Federal legislation establish broad liability upon owners and/or
users of real property for the investigation and remediation of Hazardous
Substances. The determination of the existence of a Hazardous Substance
Condition and the evaluation of the impact of such a condition are highly
technical and beyond the expertise of Brokers. The Parties acknowledge that
they have been advised by Brokers to consult their own technical and legal
experts with respect to the possible presence of Hazardous Substances on the
Property or adjoining properties, and Buyer and Seller are not relying upon any
investigation by or statement of Brokers with respect thereto. The Parties
hereby assume all responsibility for the impact of such Hazardous Substances upon
their respective interests herein.</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-18.65pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">10.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Documents Required at or before Closing:</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.1&#160; Five days prior to the Closing date Escrow
Holder shall obtain an updated Title Commitment concerning the Property from
the Title Company and provide copies thereof to each of the Parties.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.2&#160; Seller shall deliver to Escrow Holder in time
for delivery to Buyer at the Closing:</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160; Grant </font><strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">or general warranty</font></strike></font> deed <font color="red" style="color:red;">on Title Company&#146;s standard form</font>, duly executed and in recordable form,
conveying fee title to the Property to Buyer <font color="red" style="color:red;">with the documentary transfer taxes to be shown in an
off-record affidavit</font>.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160; If applicable, the Beneficiary Statements
concerning Existing Note(s).</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160; </font><strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">If applicable, the Existing Leases and Other</font></strike></font> <font color="red" style="color:red;">The Other</font>
Agreements together with duly executed assignments thereof by Seller and Buyer.
<strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">The assignment of Existing
Leases shall be on the most recent Assignment and Assumption of Lessor&#146;s
Interest in Lease form published by the AIR or its equivalent</font></strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">.&#160; A
termination of the Existing Lease between Seller as landlord and Safe
Publishing Company Inc. as tenant.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d) If applicable, Estoppel
Certificates executed by Seller and/or the tenant(s) of the Property.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e) An affidavit executed by
Seller to the effect that Seller is not a &#147;foreign person&#148; within the meaning
of Internal Revenue Code Section 1445 or successor statutes. If Seller does not
provide such affidavit in form reasonably satisfactory to Buyer at least 3
business days prior to the Closing, Escrow Holder shall at the Closing deduct
from Seller&#146;s proceeds and remit to Internal Revenue Service such sum as is
required by applicable Federal law with respect to purchases from foreign
sellers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f) If the Property is
located in California, an affidavit executed by Seller to the effect that
Seller is not a &#145;&#145;nonresident&#148; within the meaning of California Revenue and Tax
Code Section 18662 or successor statutes. If Seller does not provide such

proceeds and remit to the Franchise Tax Board such sum as is required by such

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)&#160; </font><strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">If applicable, a </font></strike><font color="red" style="color:red;">A</font></font>
bill of sale, duly executed, conveying title to any included personal property
to Buyer<font color="red" style="color:red;">,&#160; and also an assignment from Seller to Buyer

Seller will also provide to Buyer keys, operating manuals, etc.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><strike><font size="2" color="red" face="Times New Roman" style="color:red;font-size:10.0pt;">(h) If the Seller is a corporation, a duly
executed corporate resolution authorizing the execution of this Agreement and
the sale of the Property.</font></strike></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.3&#160; Buyer shall deliver to Seller through Escrow:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a) The cash portion of the
Purchase Price and such additional sums as are required of Buyer under this
Agreement shall be deposited by Buyer with Escrow Holder, by federal funds wire
transfer, or any other method acceptable to Escrow Holder as immediately
collectable funds, no later than 2:00 P.M. on the business day prior to the

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b) If a Purchase Money Note
and Purchase Money Deed of Trust are called for by this Agreement, the duly
executed originals of those documents, the Purchase Money Deed of Trust being
in recordable form, together with evidence of fire insurance on the

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c) The Assignment and

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d) Assumptions duly executed
by Buyer of the obligations of Seller that accrue after Closing under any Other
